# EstreGenesis Changelog

Each tier (Master / Lite / Compact) has its own version. Master is the authoritative evolution track; Lite and Compact are derived regularly from Master but may lag by a release.

This file is the **changelog SSoT** — each seed file keeps only a compact header metadata line with tier, language, current version, counterpart, and a pointer back to this `CHANGELOG.md`, not the target project's README. When you upgrade a project using Migration B, the agent uses the seed header version marker plus this changelog to compute the delta.

**Language**: **English** (below) · [한국어](#한국어)

---

<a id="english"></a>

## Changelog (English)

- **v1.0** (2026-04-18) — First edition (Master). Based on the author's second AI Native project.
- **v1.1** (2026-04-19) — Research → Report → Plan loop section added. Core Principle #7.
- **v1.2** (2026-04-20) — Migration A/B/C guides added. Bootstrap/Migration mode branching at top of Agent Instructions. Lite and Compact tiers initial release.
- **v1.3** (2026-05-02) — Two new core principles: #8 (Index ↔ body synchronization) and #9 (External-interface N-way sync). Six new sections: § Index Synchronization Policy · § External-Interface N-Way Sync · § Markdown Tilde Escape Policy · § RAG Index Optimization · § External Delivery Build Pipeline · § Document Inflation Prevention (appendix `<NN>b_*.md` pattern). All three tiers updated; Lite and Compact gain condensed forms of the same patterns. All additions distilled from real incidents in the author's second AI Native project's 2026-04-21 → 2026-05-02 operations: a one-week stale external-surface leak (drove the N-way sync policy), a last-minute markdown strikethrough in an external-delivery PDF (drove the tilde escape policy), another agent acting on a stale index (drove the index sync policy), and a project file capacity hitting 100% in a Claude project workspace (drove the RAG-friendly indexing rules).
- **v1.3.1** (2026-05-02) — Self-sufficient tooling: master seed § File Templates now embeds full inline scripts so the seed bootstraps a complete external-delivery toolchain without external references. New templates: `scripts/escape-md-tildes.mjs` (no-deps Node ≥18, idempotent, placeholder-protected algorithm), `scripts/build-md-to-html.mjs` (`marked`-based MD → A4 HTML with h2 page-break, project-language font stack), and convenience wrappers `scripts/build-pdf.ps1` (Windows) / `scripts/build-pdf.sh` (macOS/Linux) that chain the 3-step `escape → HTML → Chrome --print-to-pdf` pipeline. § Markdown Tilde Escape Policy gains an "Algorithm" subsection explaining why placeholder-based protection is mandatory (vs. naïve regex). § External Delivery Build Pipeline gains a "Why these specific tools" subsection (`marked` vs Puppeteer trade-offs, A4 page rules) and macOS/Linux Chrome equivalents. Lite and Compact tiers expand their § Markdown `~` Escape (condensed) sections with the placeholder algorithm summary and the cross-platform PDF pipeline; the master seed remains the single source for the inline scripts.
- **v1.3.2** (2026-05-02) — `.gitignore` template + cross-tier audit. **`.gitignore`**: Master § File Templates now embeds an inline template — Common (OS, IDE, env, logs) + per-stack rows for Node / Python / Go / Rust / JVM / C-C++ / Mobile / DB + a Seed-produced artifacts block using a `.generated.` infix convention so the rule precisely sweeps build outputs without trapping handcrafted attachments. **Cross-tier audit**: the README's stated principle ("each tier is self-contained — internally complete, no forward or backward references to other tiers") had been violated since v1.0; the v1.3.1 release made it worse by adding more cross-tier references. v1.3.2 brings the **Lite** and **Compact** tiers back into compliance — every "→ master seed § ..." cross-reference removed. Lite is now 909 / 912 lines (Korean / English) with a complete § File Templates section embedding inline AGENTS.md, `.agent/rules.md`, `.gitignore` (Common + Phase 2 stacks + seed artifacts), `scripts/escape-md-tildes.mjs` (compressed Node ≥18), `scripts/build-md-to-html.mjs` (compressed `marked` + A4 CSS), and stubs for all 11 supported AI service bridges. Compact is 119 lines per language with a new § Scaffold specs section providing algorithm-spec descriptions for each scaffold target — the agent reads the spec and generates the actual files. All three tiers now ship independently into a project repo as the README has always promised.
- **v1.3.4** (2026-05-03) — Enforcement Hook Architecture added. Master gains a full section describing two-layer enforcement: Layer 1 Claude Code `PreToolUse` plus Layer 2 `git pre-commit`, both backed by a single regex SSoT in `scripts/hooks/_patterns.mjs`; an idempotent installer creates the `.git/hooks/pre-commit` shim and merges `.claude/settings.local.json`; path matching, Bash quote/HEREDOC false-positive handling, tests, and cross-AI applicability are documented. Lite gets a condensed version, and Compact adds Principle #10 plus a sync-rules bullet.
- **v1.3.5** (2026-05-03) — Task Decomposition Strategy added. The seed now gives agents a cross-AI pattern for complex work with multiple decomposition paths: announce the chosen shape, proceed by judgment/inertia without stalling for confirmation, and accept explicit or implicit user pivots mid-flight. Master includes thresholds, inertia priority, per-AI tool mapping, and anti-patterns; Lite and Compact carry condensed forms.
- **v1.3.6** (2026-05-03) — External knowledge index auto-sync added under Index ↔ Body Sync. When a project mirrors structured folders into an external KB such as Claude memory, Notion, a wiki, or RAG metadata, pre-commit may call a dedicated sync script to update mechanical structure (counts, stubs, numbering, orphan warnings) while leaving semantic content human-curated. Master has the full subsection; Lite and Compact carry condensed clauses.
- **v1.3.7** (2026-05-03) — Phase 0 now captures agent reply tone after working language. Korean prompts offer six speech-level choices (`~니다`, `~에요/예요/어요`, `~음/슴/임`, casual peer tone, blunt challenge tone, or custom direction); English prompts carry equivalent tone choices. Default is to match the user's opening tone or use one notch more polite. Generated `AGENTS.md`, `.agent/rules.md`, and bridge stubs now record language and tone separately.
- **v1.4.0** (2026-05-03) — Applied the official EstreGenesis naming across document titles, anonymized source-project references for public release, and published the seed prompt library as a public repo. Content base: legacy private archive, commit `5944a50` (v1.3.6, 2026-05-03).
- **v1.4.1** (2026-05-06) — Metadata reconciliation. During the v1.3.6 → v1.4.0 absorption pass, the Master tier (KO/EN) Migration B delta tables omitted the v1.3.4 (Enforcement Hook Architecture), v1.3.5 (Task Decomposition Strategy), and v1.3.6 (External knowledge index auto-sync) rows that the four other tiers carried. v1.4.0 content is unchanged — the three rows are reinstated to restore 6-tier sync. The Master Phase 7 § File Scaffolding Checklist also gains an explicit optional `scripts/hooks/` block (Enforcement Hook Architecture is opt-in for projects with absolute rules worth enforcing). README v1.4.0 entry gains the legacy archive SHA for traceability.
- **v1.5.0** (2026-05-07) — Bootstrap Residency added across all six seed files. New Phase 2.5 decides whether the workspace is a source repo, private agent-docs sidecar, multi-project orchestration repo, or upstream/local split before choosing `<scope-root>`. It supports Minimal, Full manual, and repo-provider assisted bootstrap (GitHub, GitLab, Bitbucket, Azure DevOps, Gitea, Forgejo, self-hosted/local remotes, or user-provided repo lists), adds workspace-limited-agent warnings, defaults upstream folders to `upstream/` unless renamed by the user, and guards `.gitignore` sidecar-source entries with explicit user identification plus agent verification. Master also gains an Adoption Catalog with trigger conditions; Lite and Compact carry condensed forms.
- **v1.5.1** (2026-05-08) — Patch release from adoption feedback. All six seed headers now clarify that the changelog pointer means the **upstream EstreGenesis repository README.md**, not the target project's README.md after the seed is copied. KO Master also fixes v1.5.0 absorption leftovers: Phase 0 and Phase 4 closing lines now correctly point to Phase 7, the new Phase 2.5 sub-headings are localized, and the Adoption Catalog heading/table header are localized.
- **v1.6.0** (2026-05-09) — Agent-time vs human-time estimation. AI agents that estimate using human dev-team baselines inflate plans 5–10×, which causes calendar mismatches and erodes PM template usefulness. Phase 0 now asks one more question after language and tone: **execution pace mode** — Cautious 2–4× (free tier or local LLM like Continue.dev / Aider with local models, calibrated against output tokens-per-second), Proactive 5–6× (default for paid plans), Burst 6–8× (high-throughput plans), Sprint 9–10× (effectively unlimited tokens, max parallelism). Within each mode, task type adjusts the position: execution-heavy work hits the top, debugging the middle, research / strategy stays at ~1× regardless because human review is rate-limiting. Every duration estimate splits **agent active time** from **human review / approval time** plus a **calendar window** that absorbs handoff gaps. Mode is project-wide and switchable mid-project ("switch to sprint" / "drop to cautious") with automatic re-baselining of active PM estimates and a CHANGELOG entry. The seed self-calibrates against actuals: ±30%+ deltas log to `.agent/_lessons/` with the `estimation` tag, and after three+ such entries in the same mode the agent proposes a calibrated multiplier. Master gains Core Principle #11 plus a full § Agent-Time Estimation Policy section (two-axis framework, mode-switch protocol, self-calibration loop, anti-patterns, cross-AI applicability). Lite carries Principle #8 plus a condensed policy section. Compact carries Principle #13 inline. PM templates across all tiers updated to the split-time format. AGENTS.md Core rules line 1 now records language + tone + pace mode together.
- **v2.0.0** (2026-05-27) — Adds **Constellation** (Core Principle #12 / Lite #9 / Compact #14), one optional module. Multi-agent coordination graduates from the file-based `.agent/_coordination/` ledger to a real-time live board (WebSocket + A2A messaging + dashboard). The **A2A bridge interface** (roles board/main/local/upstream/collab · handshake · messaging · turn-based bridge-daemon + self-wake-watcher runtime pattern) is the invariant contract; adoption depth follows the seed tier. Constellation ships as a separate `Constellation.md` guide + `constellation/*.eux` component specs — including `gateway-client.eux`, the detail-tier A2A adapter — referenced from the tier seeds by raw GitHub URL so the seeds stay lean. Its live-board UI components are authored as `.eux` and brewed with **EstreUX**, a separate runtime EstreGenesis *references* (not bundles or owns); EstreGenesis does not own or teach the EUX format — it is a build-time dependency of Constellation, not a layer of the seed. File-based coordination (Phase 5) remains the default. The prior v1.6.0 state is preserved on the `1.x` branch; 2.0 is `main`. Constellation matures toward a published EstreGenesis Claude plugin.
- **v2.1.0** (2026-05-28) — **Constellation runtime distillation + self-sufficiency.** The live-board runtime is now distilled into public `.eux` so any project can build a compatible board without access to a private reference runtime: `constellation/server.eux` (deps-0 HTTP + WS router — agent registry, role classification, A2A relay with reply-window pairing, telemetry exclusion, graceful main handoff, per-channel history), `local-bridge.eux` (file-IO control/A2A bridge for turn-based agents), `self-wake-watcher.eux` (infinite-wait self-wake), and `watchdog.eux` (server/bridge liveness guard). `Constellation.md` is made **self-sufficient** — the orchestration protocol and infinite-wait methodology are distilled inline (A2A reply-envelope, telemetry exclusion, handshake order), private file citations removed, and the **watch-state invariant** (an agent joined to a board never ends its conversation — always re-arm the watcher and return to watch) + re-arm duty + watch-state discipline strengthened. **EstreUX brew-runtime reference** clarified end to end: repo URL + clone-and-run brew CLI (`node bin/estreux.mjs brew`) added to `Constellation.md §6` and `constellation/README.md` (replacing a private reference-client citation), and a one-line EstreUX pointer propagated to all six seed tiers so a migrating agent can locate the runtime. EstreUX remains a referenced Apache-2.0 build dependency, not bundled or owned. Drafts distilled by the EstreGenesis agent from on-disk runtime sources and precision-reviewed by the upstream live-board main.
- **v2.1.1** (2026-05-28) — EstreUX brew-runtime reference sync. EstreUX published `v0.1.0` (deps-0 ~21 KB engine, files-whitelisted), so the references added in v2.1.0 are updated from "clone-and-run, not an npm package" to the recommended lightweight **giget** fetch (`npx giget gh:SoliEstre/EstreUX/spike#v0.1.0 ./estreux-engine` → `node ./estreux-engine/expand.mjs brew <comp>.eux`), with full-clone (`bin/estreux.mjs`) and a publish-ready npm package noted as alternatives. Synced across `Constellation.md §6`, `constellation/README.md`, and the EstreUX pointer in all six seed tiers; trimmed a duplicate EstreUX mention in the Compact tiers.
- **v2.2.0** (2026-05-28) — **Constellation reference master copies.** Adds `constellation/reference/` for downstreams that want a fully-working baseline alongside the rough/detail `.eux` specs: `state-schema.md` (the board SSoT data model — `state.json` top-level + task tracks `current/done/planned` + decisions panel + free request + per-channel history + keys + feedback, with the generic-PM vs domain-specific boundary made explicit) and `dashboard/` (a vanilla DOM master copy `index.html` · `style.css` · `app.js` generalized from a working private implementation, renders `state.json` per the schema; copy and re-skin per stack). The §2 A2A bridge interface remains the only byte-identical invariant; reference copies are concrete starting points, not contracts. `gateway/` and `runtime/` reference master copies are planned for post-v2.2.0 patches (drift managed by periodic re-distillation). Diagnosed from an observed downstream migration where rough-tier brewing produced only a ping/pong-level board — the gap was "what to render?" (data model), not "how to render?" (UI design). Drafted by the EstreGenesis agent and precision-reviewed by the upstream live-board main.
- **v2.3.0** (2026-05-29) — **Superscalar module + autonomous-execution absolute principle.** Two new Core Principles (Master #13/#14, Lite #10/#11, Compact #15/#16): (1) **Execution scheduling (Superscalar, optional referenced module)** bounds `issue_width` by five dimensions (Anthropic effort band · pace_mode cap · Little's Law throughput · Kanban WIP · `autonomy_available_workers`) with cost-benefit-gated dispatch (~30-60k token-horizon crossover); (2) **Autonomous execution (absolute)** — defined-next-step (Phase ordering · `planned` track · `blocked` clearance · in-order retire queue) proceeds without asking, gating only on (a) loss / external publish, (b) new major branch decision-point (RRP / design — at the *decision point* only; the resulting Phase A/B/C plan is *decided execution*), (c) restart-requiring deploys (apply autonomously, coordinate the *restart timing* only), (d) explicit user steering. Phase 0 gains a fourth question (`execution scheduling: serial/parallel` + `speculation: off/on`); AGENTS.md template § 5 Core rules line 1 becomes the Autonomous execution rule. Master adds a new § Execution Scheduling section that references `Superscalar.md` (same module-reference pattern as § Constellation); Lite/Compact carry compressed in-principle references. Consolidates the v2.2.x patch series under one anchor: **v2.2.1** (Hermes gateway reference master copy), **v2.2.2** (`constellation/reference/gateway/main` + `runtime/` references — Node deps-0 generic adapter), **v2.2.3** (upstream live-board Report 2 fixes — A2A classifier · `AgentHello` shape literal · cursor unit drift), **v2.2.4** (Report 2 follow-up — server-stamped truth · leniency-WARN · role hint vs truth · runtime liveness). Superscalar Stage 1 dogfood baseline (`Superscalar.md §11` Entry 01-03 on Phase C reference work) ships stable; the `autonomy_available_workers` dimension and Andon worker-autonomy precheck were added from dogfood telemetry showing Haiku-tier worker unfit for autonomous lane (per-dispatch permission prompts collapse throughput). Drafted by the EstreGenesis agent with upstream live-board main co-review (Delegate seq 119 dogfood telemetry + seq 123 absolute-principle pin).
- **v2.5.36** (2026-06-03) — **`docs/promo` sweep: module order (Superscalar → Hyperbrief → Constellation) across nav + index card; new install section in `docs/hyperbrief.html` + `docs/superscalar.html` (matching the pattern `docs/constellation.html` has carried since v2.5.16); new `.nav a.sub-link` CSS class makes the per-page Spec entry visually attach as a sub-entry of the active page (↳ glyph + dotted leader + muted tint + smaller font); `docs/index.html` 24h-dogfood section reframed as "the first 24 hours" historical snapshot + new "Since then" cumulative metrics; `docs/shared/data.js` meta v2.5.25 → v2.5.36; per-module hero badges + meta descriptions caught up to current frontmatter versions; Adoption / Read-more sections updated to reflect the shipped Constellation §13.16.9 + Superscalar §3.1 cross-module integrations.** Public-site sweep cut. The promo site had carried a stale module ordering (Super → Constell → Hyper, reflecting the chronological addition order at v2.5.26) and an outdated "Adoption section" prose for Hyperbrief that still flagged the cross-module integrations as "queued follow-ups" despite both being shipped at v2.5.27 + v2.5.29. The Superscalar promo page had never carried an install section (only Constellation did, since v2.5.16). This cut closes all five visibility/ordering items in a single sweep + adds the per-page sub-link styling. **Module ordering** — `docs/index.html` Modules card grid + all 4 promo page nav bars (`docs/index.html` / `docs/superscalar.html` / `docs/hyperbrief.html` / `docs/constellation.html`) rewritten to `Superscalar → Hyperbrief → Constellation` ordering (the seed-version pivot grouping the three modules by their relative position in the stack: Superscalar = execution scheduling, Hyperbrief = decision delegation, Constellation = orchestration / communication). The index Modules card swap also tightens cross-module references in card prose: the Hyperbrief card now mentions `Constellation §13.16.9 + Superscalar §3.1 integrations shipped`; the Constellation card mentions the Hyperbrief A2A-intent family + ack_tier='decided' extension. **`docs/hyperbrief.html` install section** — new "Try it yourself" / "Install the plugin" / "Plugin deployment" section (3-tier audience) modeled on `docs/constellation.html`'s pattern: 3-tier prose + `<pre><code>` block with `/plugin marketplace add SoliEstre/EstreGenesis` + `/plugin install hyperbrief@estregenesis-plugins` + optional `HYPERBRIEF_LEDGER_PATH` env override + final paragraph noting Hyperbrief is self-contained (no external infra required) with optional Constellation + Superscalar synergies. **`docs/superscalar.html` install section** — new install section modeled on the same pattern: 3-tier prose + `/plugin install superscalar@estregenesis-plugins` + explicit "0 npm deps / 0 env" callout + optional hyperbrief co-install hint to activate the v0.4.1 §3.1 interlock end-to-end; the "Read more" section is also updated to list §3.1 alongside the existing §1-§5 + §11 anchors. **`docs/hyperbrief.html` Adoption section update** — prose rewritten to reflect that Constellation §13.16.9 + Superscalar §3.1 integrations are **shipped** (previously "queued follow-ups"); plugin bundle description updated to include the four-tool MCP server + FullBrief + BlockedStub template variants (2 → 4 templates). Hero badges updated `v0.4.1 → v0.5.2` + `23 anti-patterns → 26 anti-patterns` + `2 dogfood entries → 2 dogfood + adopter bundle` + new `4 MCP tools` badge. Meta description rewritten with `(FullBrief + BlockedStub)` IR variant + `21 MUST / 8 SHOULD` + `4 MCP tools` + `Constellation §13.16.9 + Superscalar §3.1 integrations shipped`. **`docs/superscalar.html` hero badges** — `v0.4 → v0.4.2` + `§11 Entry 01-06 → §11 Entry 01-06 (n=8)` + new `§3.1 Hyperbrief interlock` badge. Meta description updated `Superscalar v0.4 → Superscalar v0.4.2` + new `§3.1 Hyperbrief decision-delegation interlock` clause + `Plugin v0.1.2` reference. **`docs/constellation.html` hero badges** — `v2.5.15 → v2.3.21` (frontmatter version, more accurate than the EG tag previously displayed) + new `§13.16.9 Hyperbrief intents` + `bundle 007 absorbed` badges. Meta description rewritten to enumerate §13.9.1 / §13.9.2 / §13.16.9 + the Hyperbrief decision-delegation A2A intents + bundle 007 absorption. **`.nav a.sub-link` CSS class** (new, `docs/shared/shared.css`) — applied to the per-page Spec entry on all three module pages so the Spec link visually attaches as a sub-entry of the active page rather than reading as a peer top-level item. Style: 0.82rem font + 0.72 opacity + `↳ ` prefix glyph + dotted left border leader + negative left margin to attach to the preceding active link; hover restores full opacity. Adopters reading the nav at a glance can see at-a-glance that the Spec is a deeper link off the current page, not a separate destination. **`docs/index.html` 24h-dogfood section** — section headings reframed from "What we made in 24 hours" → "What we made in the first 24 hours" (with `(24h)` clarifier on the Tagged releases metric); 3-tier preamble explaining the snapshot is historical (predates Hyperbrief module ship + bundle absorption); new "Since then" / "Cumulative since the 24h baseline" / "Cumulative state since the initial baseline" sub-section with 3-tier prose + 4 cumulative metrics (~21 post-baseline cuts · 3 adopter bundles absorbed · 1 new optional module · 2 cross-module integrations shipped). **`docs/shared/data.js`** meta `version: 'v2.5.15' → 'v2.5.36'` + `shipCount: 31 → 52`. **`docs/index.html` hero badges** — `v2.5.25 → v2.5.36` + `Hyperbrief v0.4.1 → Hyperbrief v0.5.2`. **Scope discipline**: 4 promo HTML pages (index + superscalar + hyperbrief + constellation) + `docs/shared/shared.css` (CSS rule addition) + `docs/shared/data.js` (meta version bumps). No spec body changes. No plugin source changes. No schema changes. No renderer changes. No seed lib changes. No reference runtime changes. No wire format changes. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — public-site sync for shipped module integrations + new install sections + ordering pivot is a minor cut, mirrors v2.5.26's docs(promo) Hyperbrief entry pattern.
- **v2.5.35** (2026-06-03) — **Seed lib v2.4.1 → v2.4.2 — Migration B dual-track guidance per bundle 007 M1: Step 1 (Identify starting version) + Step 2 (Diff capabilities) now explicitly describe the seed-version vs EG-release-version separation and require cross-checking BOTH markers before declaring a starting state. Cascades across all 6 seed tiers (Master + Lite + Compact × EN/KO).** Seed-lib cut. Bundle 007 M1 surfaced a 2-track tracking gap: the seed-version marker (e.g., `v2.4.1`, embedded in `AGENTS.md`) and the EG-release version (e.g., `v2.5.x`, advancing on every meaningful push per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md`) are independent — a release-only cut (e.g., Constellation `§13.x` patch, Hyperbrief module ship) does NOT bump the seed version, so a migrating adopter that checks only the seed marker may conclude "no delta" when substantial module/spec changes have landed. The fix is a Migration B Step 1 + Step 2 rewrite (Master tier full, Lite tier condensed, Compact tier 1-liner) that makes the dual-track expectation explicit. **Master tier (Master EN + Master KO)** — Step 1 expanded from one paragraph to a structured sub-section naming the two tracks ("seed version" vs "EG release version") + a "Check both markers before declaring a starting version" paragraph explaining the failure mode + cross-check sources (AGENTS.md seed marker + adoption manifest EG-release + upstream `CHANGELOG.md` HEAD) + revised user-question wording ("which EG release tag was current at that time?"). Step 2 prefaced with "List X for the starting **seed version** (table below), AND list Y for the starting **release version** (consult upstream `CHANGELOG.md` between the two release tags — typically a `git log <starting-tag>..HEAD --oneline -- CHANGELOG.md` against the EG repo, or just read the CHANGELOG entries between the two tags)" and the existing seed-delta table is now labeled "Seed-delta table" so readers know it's only one of the two tracks. **Lite tier (Lite EN + Lite KO)** — condensed equivalent: Step 1 carries the dual-track explanation in 2 sentences + cross-check instruction; Step 2 prefaced with the dual-track diff. **Compact tier (Compact EN + Compact KO)** — 1-liner extension at the start of Step 1 + 1-liner reframe of Step 2 ("diff capabilities (both tracks)"). **Frontmatter version markers** — all 6 tier headers bump `version: v2.4.1 → v2.4.2` + `date: 2026-05-31 → 2026-06-03` + status fragment `v2.4.2 = bundle 007 M1 reflection — Migration B Step 1/2 dual-track guidance` (Master) / condensed forms (Lite + Compact). **Why a seed bump (rather than just a CHANGELOG note)** — the change is to the seed body itself (Migration B procedure), not to a referenced module — adopters bootstrapping new projects from this seed cut get the dual-track guidance built into the Migration B section, not as an out-of-band CHANGELOG cross-reference. The seed-version marker was unchanged since v2.4.1 (2026-05-31) because the prior cuts (v2.5.0 through v2.5.34) were all release-track changes that did not touch the seed body — this is the first true seed-body change since v2.4.1, validating the 2-track separation that the change itself codifies. **Cross-tier consistency check passes** — the dual-track guidance is now present in all 6 tiers; the substance is identical (two tracks, cross-check both, ask user which EG release tag was current); the verbosity scales per tier (Master = full prose explanation, Lite = 2 sentences, Compact = 1 line). **Scope discipline**: 6 seed-tier files (Master EN + Master KO + Lite EN + Lite KO + Compact EN + Compact KO) — each gets Migration B Step 1 and Step 2 prefix updates + frontmatter version bump. No module changes (Constellation.md / Superscalar.md / Hyperbrief.md untouched). No plugin changes. No reference runtime changes. No schema changes. No renderer changes. No docs/promo changes. No wire format changes. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — seed-body change is a minor cut; mirrors v2.5.0's seed cascade pattern (v2.3.0 Superscalar/autonomous-execution principles) but smaller scope (Step 1+2 sub-section + 6 frontmatter, not new sections). Closes the bundle 007 M1 ask; the bundle 007 absorption ledger is now fully reflected across v2.5.32 (H1) + v2.5.33 (F1–F7 + M2) + v2.5.34 (M4) + v2.5.35 (M1).
- **v2.5.34** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.1 → v0.5.2 refinements + bundle 008 promote (`_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/`): H2 status-based template selection + new compact BlockedStub templates / H3 self-contained `--help` clarity / H5 essence_one_line heading-strip / H6 plugin README catch-up sync / M4 new §8.5 sub-section codifying Hyperbrief's relation to Constellation §13.17 (main-chat structured-choice prohibition) and §13.18 (autonomous-execution absolute principle).** Bundle 008 absorption sweep. The downstream adopter's Hyperbrief-adoption dogfooding bundle (the H1 blocker landed as v2.5.32) ships the remaining 4 refinements + 1 cross-module clarification with no further blockers. **Bundle promoted** — `assets/reports/2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/` (staging) → `_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/` (tracked) per staging note's "bundle 합류 또는 별도 bundle"; the bundle ships with `001_findings.md` (H1–H6 detailed + positives + 우선순위 권고) and a Korean `README.md`. **H2** (Med, code + templates) — `mini-engine.cjs` previously rendered every IR through `brief.{md,html}.template` regardless of the IR's `status` field, so a `BlockedStub` IR (`status: 'blocked_low_escalation'` — agent decided autonomously) rendered through the `FullBrief` template, producing empty fields for `Reversibility / Decider / Recommender / Deadline / Reading time` AND an irrelevant "⚠ Low-confidence brief" banner (the BlockedStub has neither those fields nor the `epistemic_distribution` the banner reads). Schema declares `oneOf [FullBrief, BlockedStub]` but the renderer ignored the variant. Two new templates `templates/brief-stub.md.template` + `templates/brief-stub.html.template` (compact post-notify card — escalation 4-score + sum + `autonomy_refusal_reason` + `autonomous_action_taken` + `post_notify_message`; one-screen surface; explanatory footer guiding how to force a FullBrief if needed). New `selectTemplate(ir, surface)` function picks the correct template based on `ir.status === 'blocked_low_escalation'`. Smoke test confirms BlockedStub renders the compact card (epistemic tag `[verified]` correctly transformed to `확인됨 —` at audience L2; determinism PASS on both surfaces — `md run1==run2 = f1e912d0aff8ea39`, `html run1==run2 = 202c9e5e5257270d`). **H3** (Low, CLI) — `bin/render.cjs --help` previously advertised `--self-contained` without indicating its v0.4.3-deferred status; the flag was a no-op that only logged a stderr warning ("inline asset bundling is deferred"). The `--help` string now reads `--self-contained (deferred to v0.4.3 — emits stderr warning, output still references CDN)` so adopters reading `--help` know it's not yet effective. Hard-fail considered but rejected — many adopters set the flag preemptively as a stylistic preference, and silent-deferred-warn preserves their workflow without forcing them to remove and re-add the flag at v0.4.3. **H5** (Low, renderer) — `section_6_decision_prompt.essence_one_line` carries the canonical epistemic-tag prefix (`[verified|inferred|assumed|unknown]`) in the IR (it's a `tagged_text` per `§5.1`), but the rendered MD H1 heading received that tag verbatim — e.g., `# ADR-hb-... — [verified] 결정 위임을 ...`. The tag is doughnut-chart metadata, not heading content. New `stripHeadingEpistemicTag(ir)` runs at the start of `renderMd` and `renderHtml` and strips the canonical bracket form (and the optional provenance bracket form) from `essence_one_line` only. The IR's field is mutated (per the §5.6.6 surface-vs-field separation), but `epistemic_distribution` and AF-18 estimate read from other fields, so the chart-tier signals are unaffected. **H6** (Low, doc) — `plugins/hyperbrief/README.md` was historically "Phase 1 prototype (v0.1.0)" — the v2.5.28 cut bumped `plugin.json` to v0.4.2 (and v2.5.30 to v0.5.0, v2.5.32 to v0.5.1) without touching the README. The README is now rewritten as `# Hyperbrief plugin — Phase 2 production (v0.5.2)` with a top-of-file callout noting the historic drift and the v0.5.2 catch-up; the "무엇을 주는가" section now describes the deterministic Node renderer + MCP server (both shipped at Phase 2) + the new BlockedStub templates; "Infrastructure requirements" reframed from "Phase 2 will add the renderer" to "renderers + mcp both shipped + single ajv ^8.17.0 dep" + active Constellation §13.16.9 / Superscalar §3.1 synergies. **M4** (Med, cross-module) — `Hyperbrief.md` gains new sub-section §8.5 "Constellation autonomous-execution layer — relation to §13.17 / §13.18" that codifies the boundaries between the three sections: §13.17 = first-move surface (no forced menus on contact); §13.18 = autonomous-execution absolute principle (gating conditions enumerated); Hyperbrief = post-§13.18-pass structured brief (output discipline once gating fires). The three cover disjoint surfaces — §13.18's four gating conditions map to Hyperbrief's MUST-trigger conditions, and §13.18 governs whether to ask while Hyperbrief governs how to ask once the answer is "yes, ask". Closes the bundle 007 M4 ask ("Constellation §13.17/§13.18 과의 중첩 범위를 어댑터가 직접 매핑해야 함") — adopters no longer need to derive the cross-section boundaries themselves. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.1 → v0.5.2` + status string rewritten to list the 5 refinements + bundle 008 absorption attribution. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.1 → 0.5.2` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Scope discipline**: 2 new templates (`brief-stub.md.template` + `brief-stub.html.template`) + `mini-engine.cjs` (3 small functions: `stripHeadingEpistemicTag` + `selectTemplate` + each render entry-point's 2-line additions) + `bin/render.cjs` (1-line `--help` change) + `plugins/hyperbrief/README.md` (full rewrite to catch up Phase 2 surface) + `Hyperbrief.md` (§8.5 new sub-section + frontmatter) + version bumps (1 plugin manifest + 2 package.json + 1 frontmatter) + new `_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/{001_findings.md, README.md}`. - **v2.5.32** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.0 → v0.5.1 emergency-fix — clean-install ajv blocker (bundle 007 H1): `mini-engine.cjs` + `mcp/server.cjs` ajv import switched from default draft-07 entrypoint (`require("ajv")`) to draft-2020-12 dialect entrypoint (`require("ajv/dist/2020")`). Determinism PASS re-verified post-fix.** 2-line emergency-fix release. Bundle 007 (Hyperbrief adoption dogfooding from a downstream adopter) surfaced a blocker: `ajv` 8.x default export is the draft-07 dialect, but `hyperbrief.schema.json` declares `"$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema"` — so `ajv.compile(schema)` throws `no schema with key or ref draft/2020-12/schema` on every IR, breaking the validation-on default code path entirely. The adopter could render only with `--skip-validate`; shipped packages installed via `npm install` could not validate at all. The v0.4.0 determinism smoke test PASSED because it was run with `--skip-validate` against an already-vendored older ajv resolution; clean-install adopters did not have that escape. **The fix** is the 1-line import change per file (×2 files: renderers + mcp), with an inline comment explaining why the default draft-07 entrypoint is wrong for this schema's dialect. **Reproduction**: smoke test re-run with real `ajv ^8.17.0` installed in a clean node_modules confirms (a) compile no longer throws, (b) validation-on render proceeds normally, (c) IR-content schema enforcement now catches per-field violations as designed (the test ran against a sample IR with deliberate epistemic-tag gaps, ajv flagged each at correct path); determinism re-verified PASS (`md run1==run2` byte-identical, `html run1==run2` byte-identical — hashes match v0.5.0 post-button-label baseline). **Why a separate cut rather than folding into v2.5.33/.34**: H1 is a clean-install blocker for every adopter pulling EG @ v2.5.30; folding it into a larger Constellation/Hyperbrief refinement sweep would delay the fix availability. The bundle 007 + bundle 006 absorption sweeps follow as v2.5.33 + v2.5.34. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.0 → v0.5.1` + status string rewritten to flag the v0.4.0 smoke harness gap (smoke ran with `--skip-validate`, missed this) and the v0.5.1 emergency-fix cut ahead of bundle 007 absorption. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.0 → 0.5.1` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Scope discipline**: 2-line code change (renderers/mini-engine.cjs + mcp/server.cjs, each 1 import line + a one-line inline comment) + version bumps (1 frontmatter + 3 package.jsons) + this CHANGELOG entry. - **v2.5.30** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.4.2 → v0.5.0 schema v0.5 (3 schema extensions auto-computed by renderer with determinism invariant preserved + canonical button_label parenthetical universalization for adopter localization). `SurfaceProfileEstimate` $def (declared-vs-effective drift detection — AF-18 auto-warning when `|declared - estimate| >= 2` on any axis); `RecommendedArtifact` gains `language` / `line_count` / `body_hash` sub-fields (renderer auto-stamps when absent; emits AF-24 / AF-25 / AF-26 warnings on mismatch); `AudienceProfileFallback.telemetry` opt-in phrase-learning structure (`enabled` / `log_path` / `promotion_threshold`, default off to preserve render determinism). New normative MUST-20 (artifact auto-stamping + mismatch-warns) + MUST-21 (surface_profile_estimate populate + gap warning + non-override). Mini-engine implements all heuristics (english_noun_ratio + avg_sentence_length_chars + jargon_terms_per_1000_tokens + bullet_density + first_use_gloss_present + epistemic_tag_form) + auto-stamps artifact metadata + emits warnings; determinism smoke test PASS post-additions (md run1==run2 byte-identical; html run1==run2 byte-identical). `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` default parenthetical added — `"뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘 (내가 알아들을 수 있는 말로)"` — clarifies the affordance's intent ("plain language the reader can actually parse") so adopters whose primary reader-base is not Korean understand that they should LOCALIZE the literal rather than transliterate; Hyperbrief.md §5.6.7 + MUST-19 prose extended to spell out the localization SHOULD for non-Korean adopters; `docs/hyperbrief.html` + `docs/index.html` English-tier hero / card prose rewritten from "in plain Korean" to "in plain language you can actually parse (canonical EG default localizes to plain Korean — adopters localize)" so the EN audience-tier surface no longer hard-codes Korean as the affordance's only target language.** Schema + spec body cut. Hyperbrief module frontmatter `version: v0.4.2 → v0.5.0` + status string rewritten to reflect the v0.5 schema additions + determinism invariant preservation; plugin manifest `0.4.2 → 0.5.0`; sibling package.json versions (renderers + mcp) `0.4.0/0.4.2 → 0.5.0`. **`SurfaceProfileEstimate`** new $def (registered under `#/$defs`, referenced from `FullBrief.section_0_decision_header.surface_profile_estimate`): captures the renderer's estimated EFFECTIVE audience_profile from the rendered surface alongside raw metrics (`english_noun_ratio` 0-1, `avg_sentence_length_chars` int, `jargon_terms_per_1000_tokens` num, `first_use_gloss_present` bool, `bullet_density` 0-1, `epistemic_tag_form` enum `bracket|korean|superscript|mixed`) + `declared_vs_estimate_gap_warning` bool. **`RecommendedArtifact`** sub-fields added: `language` (string hint — javascript / typescript / python / json / markdown / yaml / bash / diff / etc.), `line_count` (integer, MUST equal `body.split('\n').length`), `body_hash` (sha256 hex lowercase). All three are optional in the schema but auto-stamped by the renderer when absent. **`AudienceProfileFallback.telemetry`** sub-object: `enabled` (bool, default false), `log_path` (string, default `.agent/_decisions/hyperbrief-trigger-phrase-log.jsonl`), `promotion_threshold` (int, default 3). Opt-in semantic: when enabled, adopters MAY append `confusion event` rows to a JSONL phrase-learning log; phrases recurring `>= promotion_threshold` times across distinct decision_ids are offered for promotion into the canonical `trigger_phrases_md` default set. Default off to preserve deterministic render behavior. **Mini-engine implementation**: `stampRecommendedArtifacts(ir)` walks `ir.section_8_recommendation.recommendation_conditional.recommended_artifacts[]` and auto-fills `line_count` + `body_hash` when absent (preserves user-supplied values when present); `estimateSurfaceProfile(text, declaredProfile)` runs the six heuristics (token-level english-word ratio + sentence-terminator avg length + canonical-jargon-term per-1000-token frequency + bullet-line ratio + parenthetical-gloss presence + epistemic-tag-form detection) and maps to 5-level estimated `audience`/`abbreviation`/`jargon` axes; both `renderMd` and `renderHtml` now stamp + estimate + populate `surface_profile_estimate` in the return result + emit AF-18 warning when gap `>= 2` on any axis; existing same-IR-same-options-byte-identical determinism invariant is preserved (smoke test re-run: md hash unchanged from v0.4.0 baseline `00dcf544d1975fb1`; html hash `5844d87b36d498b6 → 4a1dbaf55e8215e5` due to the button_label parenthetical change, but run1==run2 still PASS for both surfaces). **Hyperbrief.md §5.6.7-pre** new sub-section (placed between §5.6.6 epistemic-tag interaction and §5.6.7 tone-floor fallback): explains the declared-vs-effective gap that Dogfood Entry 02 surfaced, codifies the AF-18 auto-warning rule, and clarifies that heuristics are NOT authoritative (declared profile remains normative). **§5.6.7 telemetry bullet** added: spells out the opt-in adopter mechanism for phrase-learning. **§5.6.7 button-label discipline** rewritten: the canonical EG default is named verbatim (`"뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘 (내가 알아들을 수 있는 말로)"`), the parenthetical's universalization-intent is explained, and adopters serving non-Korean reader-bases are explicitly SHOULD-localized (with English / Japanese examples — `"What? Just say it plainly."` / `"何これ？私が分かる言葉で。"`). **§8 recommended_artifacts** body extended to spell out the v0.5 sub-fields + the renderer's auto-stamping behavior + the warn-on-mismatch contract. **`docs/hyperbrief.html` general-tier hero prose** rewritten: "in plain Korean" → "in plain language you can actually parse (the canonical EG default localizes to plain Korean — adopters localize the button label and trigger phrases to their reader-base)"; **`docs/index.html` Hyperbrief card general-tier prose** rewritten: "in plain Korean with a single click" → "in plain language you can parse with a single click (canonical EG default localizes to plain Korean; adopters localize)" + the EN tagline `"One-click plain-Korean re-render"` → `"One-click re-render in the reader's plain language"`. Optional machine-readable stream `.agent/_decisions/hyperbrief-ledger.jsonl` documented in the SSoT body as the append-only one-row-per-line counterpart (gitignored per EG workspace-cleanliness; reproduce locally as needed). Rationale: spec body and operational telemetry are different layers; mixing them (a) inflates the SSoT body as Entry-N grows beyond ~3 rows, (b) contaminates `git log Hyperbrief.md` with operational noise so spec-change vs ledger-append commits become indistinguishable, (c) destabilizes the file hash external adopters pin against (every Entry adds a hash delta that has nothing to do with normative spec change). **§9 archive_config layer-separation note added** — short paragraph clarifying that per-decision `archive_config` (one decision's 5-element bundle) and module-level dogfood ledger (§11.2 index over all decisions) are distinct layers; both pointer at external files but live at different granularities. **§10.2 SHOULD-8 new** — codifies the externalization rule normatively: "Module-level dogfood ledger SHOULD live in an external file, not inside the SSoT body — keep §11.2 to a recent-N-row index + pointer; full ledger at `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-ledger.md` (human) and/or `.agent/_decisions/<module>-ledger.jsonl` (machine, append-only)." with reason field. **English-normalize prose**: `Hyperbrief.md §10.3 Phase 1 transition rules` (5 numbered rules + closing paragraph + v0.4.0 status update paragraph) and `§11.3 Cross-seed adoption` (4 bullet adapter discipline + EstreUF ledger pointer paragraph) rewritten from Korean prose into English prose — Constellation.md / Superscalar.md convention parity restored (English single-language SSoT for normative body; adopters cite stable English surface). MCP tool exposure (`hyperbrief_render`) deferred to v0.4.1.** Phase 2 ship for Hyperbrief module. v0.1.1 SSoT 가 `§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules` 에서 명시했던 renderer-absent 구간을 본 cut 이 닫음 — LLM 이 더 이상 MD/HTML 을 자유형으로 작성하지 않고, JSON IR 만 emit + deterministic Node renderer 가 MD/HTML 산출. **renderer 4 파일** (`plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/`): (1) **`mini-engine.cjs` (~210 LoC)** — `canonicalIrHash` (stable JSON serialization with sorted keys at every depth → same logical IR → same hash) + `getValidator` / `validateIr` (ajv lazy load + graceful fallback when ajv not installed) + `substitute` (PLACEHOLDER_RE `\{\{([^}]+)\}\}` + auto-escape per surface) + tone axis transforms 3종 (`applyAudienceTransform` — L1-L2 epistemic bracket tags → 한국어 단어형 `확인됨 / 추론 / 가정 / 미상`, L4-L5 → superscript shorthand `ᵛ ⁱ ᵃ ᵘ`; `applyAbbreviationTransform` — L3 bullet-first, L4+ telegraphic with `vs` `→` `∵` `∴` symbolic operators; `applyJargonTransform` — L1-L2 first-occurrence gloss via `JARGON_GLOSS` dict for RAPID / Cynefin / MCDA / Toulmin / blast radius / idempotent / Hyrum) + `renderMd` / `renderHtml` 양형 + warnings 누적 + `resolveProfile` (override > IR > DEFAULT_PROFILE `{2,2,2}` with 1-5 clamp). (2) **`types.d.ts` (41 LoC)** — `AudienceProfile` `{audience, abbreviation, jargon: 1|2|3|4|5}` + `AudienceProfileFallback` + `HyperbriefIR` + `RenderResult` `{output, output_hash, ir_hash, audience_profile_applied, warnings[]}` + `RendererOptions` `{audience_profile_override?, self_contained_assets?, skip_validate?}` + `renderMd` / `renderHtml` / `canonicalIrHash` declared signatures + `McpRenderToolInput` for v0.4.1 MCP exposure. (3) **`bin/render.cjs` (~116 LoC)** — CLI entry point with `--format md|html` · `--ir <path>` (또는 stdin) · `--audience N` · `--abbreviation N` · `--jargon N` · `--self-contained` · `--skip-validate` · `--help`; exit codes 0 OK / 1 IR read failure / 2 schema validation failure / 3 unknown format; stderr emits `[warning] <msg>` for non-fatal renderer warnings. (4) **`package.json`** — name `@hyperbrief/renderers` · version `0.4.0` · private · main `./mini-engine.cjs` · types `./types.d.ts` · bin `hyperbrief-render` → `./bin/render.cjs` · single npm dep `ajv ^8.17.0` · engines `node >=18` · Apache-2.0. **Determinism smoke test (load-bearing v0.4.0 invariant per §7)**: rendering the same IR twice produces byte-identical output for both MD and HTML formats (verified — run1_hash == run2_hash for both surfaces using `bin/render.cjs --skip-validate` smoke harness). **§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained** (NOT deprecated, agent judgment per user delegation "(임시 patch 대체? 를 지금 할지는 네가 판단.)"): historical record value + 외부 adopter 가 즉시 옮겨가지 않으므로 fallback discipline 가치 지속 + Phase 1 운영 경험 보존이 향후 schema 진화 근거 + drift-log 의 의미가 "Phase 1 template-substitute output vs Phase 2 renderer output backwards-compat 회귀 검증" 으로 자연 진화. 본문 그대로 + **v0.4.0 status (2026-06-03 update)** paragraph 한 단락 추가하여 renderer ship 사실 + v0.4.0 이후 신규 brief 는 mini-engine 사용 SHOULD 명시. **Hyperbrief.md frontmatter** v0.1.1 → v0.4.0 + status 갱신 ("design draft v0.4.0 (Phase 2 — deterministic renderer shipped: plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/ mini-engine.cjs + types.d.ts + bin/render.cjs + package.json {dep: ajv ^8.17.0}; §10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained with deprecation note)"). **dogfood ledger Entry 02 적재** — decision_id `hb-20260603-r2nd02` · reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` 🟡 · outcome accept (대안 B — 자체 mini-engine + ajv + CLI; MCP tool 노출은 v0.4.1 deferred) · revisit 2026-09-01 · archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-02.md`. **Entry 02 학습 (3 schema 갭 후보 향후 patch)**: (1) Declared vs effective `audience_profile` gap — IR `audience_profile` 은 *선언* 만이고 실제 surface 가 declared level 에 부합하는지 자동 측정 지표 없음; 본 entry R1 (declared L2 / effective L3-L4 영어 jargon 비율 과다) → R2 (L1/L1/L1 재렌더) 의 근본 원인; v0.5 후보 `epistemic_distribution` 옆에 `surface_profile_estimate` (auto-computed jargon 비율 / 영어 명사 비율 / 문장 길이 평균) 추가 + declared vs estimate gap > 1.0 시 renderer warning. - **v2.5.23** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.1.0 → v0.1.1 — new optional EG module + plugin scaffold (decision-delegation gating discipline). 6-axis deep research workflow synthesis (AI harness / humanities / psychology / management / philosophy / development; 6 parallel agents → barrier synth → design → proposal authoring → scaffold; ~861k subagent tokens), self-applied as dogfood Entry 01 with 5 patches landing in v0.1.1.** New top-level module — `Hyperbrief.md` SSoT (Constellation.md / Superscalar.md 와 동일 EG-root tier, "agent → user 의사결정 위임" 직교 축 governance) + `plugins/hyperbrief/` (3 skills + IR schema + 2 templates + hooks placeholder) + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/` bundle (research bilingual + synthesis-and-design bilingual + dogfood-entry-01 박제). **Core thesis** (synthesis): Hyperbrief는 "AI가 사용자에게 결정을 묻는 행위 자체"를 규율하는 5단 파이프라인 (trigger rubric → epistemic honesty → cognitive debiasing → reversibility-first governance → learning loop closure). **JSON IR + deterministic renderer 분리** — LLM은 IR만 emit, MD/HTML drift 차단 (load-bearing). **§0 Decision Header** declares escalation 4-score + reversibility class + RAPID + Cynefin + decision_lineage + deadline + reading_minutes + stake + audience_profile (v0.1.1 신규). **§7 Decision Tree** meta-branch (accept / reject_framing / defer / request_investigation) + 3 standardized root nodes (reversibility / blast_radius / time_pressure) + Cynefin-adaptive domain format. **§10 Normative rules**: 19 MUST + 7 SHOULD. **§6 Anti-patterns**: 23 AF (16 v0.1 + 7 v0.1.1 신규). **dogfood Entry 01 (self-application)** — Hyperbrief.md v0.1 자체의 정독·승인 결정에 모듈을 적용; 사용자 결정 사이클 (sum=8/12 → FULL_HYPERBRIEF → 대안 B accept) + 사용자 추가 prompt 3건이 5 patches (P1+P2 사용자 명시 + P3+P4+P5 사용자 보완 요청)로 변환되어 v0.1.1 SSoT에 합류. **v0.1.1 patches**: (P1) **§11.3 cross-seed adoption** — EstreUF 같은 EG-seed fork 어댑터의 `hb-uf-` / `hb-eg-` decision_id 네임스페이스 + 장부 분리 + A2A 인텐트 공유 + schema 버전 고정 규율. (P2) **§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules** — v0.1.x ~ v0.4.0 renderer-absent 구간의 template-substitute 모드 운영 규칙 (IR-first invariant 유지 + 템플릿 substitution 강제 + drift-log telemetry + 톤 프로파일 적용 + self-throttle 계속 작동). (P3) **§8 recommended_artifacts[] schema slot** (load-bearing) — 사용자가 첫 브리핑에서 "patch 본문이 어디 있어?" 라고 surface한 구조적 갭을 closes; 권장안에 첨부될 artifact body를 IR에 강제 슬롯화 `{artifact_type: patch|spec|code|design|config|other, target_file, target_anchor, body, rationale_one_line}` + MUST-18 + AF-20. (P4) **§5.6 audience_profile 3축 × 5단계 + §5.6.7 tone-floor fallback affordance** — 사용자가 첫 브리핑이 "전혀 눈에 안 들어와" 라고 피드백 → audience (L1 general / L2 general-dev mid default / L3 dev / L4 dev-expert mid / L5 expert-academic) · abbreviation (L1 full sentences / L2 light compression default / L3 bullet-heavy / L4 telegraphic / L5 spec-density) · jargon (L1 no jargon / L2 1-line gloss on first use default / L3 free / L4 framework cited / L5 terse citations) 3 orthogonal axes (collapse into single complexity score 금지). **Tone-floor fallback** = HTML 항상 노출 버튼 ("뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘") + MD trigger phrases (`뭔 소리`, `안 읽혀`, `무슨 말`, `이해 안`, `더 쉽게`, `너무 어렵`, `다시 풀어`, `쉽게 다시`, `한국어로`, `한국말로`, `level 2 라고`, `L2 라고`, `이게 level`, `이게 L`) 자동 감지 시 `{1,1,1}` 재렌더. (P5) **§9 archive_config** (옵션, default ON) — 결정 캡처 시 5-element bundle (brief_original.md + decision.json + related_user_prompts.md + recommended_artifacts_applied.md + meta_learnings.md) 박제; archive_path 기본 `.agent/_decisions/<id>.archive/` 또는 `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-entry-NN.md` (proposals-tracked). **추가 anti-patterns**: AF-17 (audience_profile missing/out-of-range) · AF-18 (surface vocab mismatch profile) · AF-19 (3 tone axes collapsed) · AF-20 (recommendation cites artifact but body missing) · AF-21 (HTML brief without tone-floor button) · AF-22 (MD brief: user confusion trigger but no regen) · AF-23 (decision archived but follow-up prompts not captured). **추가 normative rules**: MUST-16 (audience_profile 필수 + 1-5 범위) · MUST-17 (3 axes orthogonality) · MUST-18 (recommendation artifact disclosure) · MUST-19 (tone-floor fallback affordance) · SHOULD-5/6/7 (tone profile chip + abbreviation-aware prose style + jargon-aware glossing). **Workflow synthesis insight** (원안 8섹션 → v0.1.1 9섹션 + IR + 5-stage pipeline): 6축 통합이 원안의 "MD/HTML 양식 출력 강제" 패턴이 representation drift를 유발한다고 식별 → schema-enforced JSON IR + deterministic renderer 분리로 진화. 본질 기능을 "결정을 잘 내리게 돕는다" → "에이전트가 사용자를 동의 강요 회로(sycophantic over-delegation loop)에 끌어들이는 것을 구조적으로 차단" 으로 재정의. **dogfood ledger Entry 01 적재** — decision_id `hb-20260603-a1b2c3` · reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` 🟡 · outcome accept (대안 B + 5 patches) · revisit 2026-09-01 · archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-01.md`. **Renderer (변환 도구) deferred to v2.5.24 (Phase 2 cut)** — 본 cut은 v0.1.1 SSoT + schema + skills + templates + dogfood archive까지; deterministic Node renderer (`renderers/`) + MCP tool 노출은 별도 ship. **Scope discipline**: 신규 모듈 + 플러그인 + proposal bundle 한정. Constellation.md 본문 unchanged (v0.2.0 cut에서 §13.16.9 allowlist에 `DECISION_REQUEST/RESPONSE/DEFER/REJECT_FRAMING/HyperbriefCard` 5개 추가 예정).
